[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No legitimate purpose**: GZIP decompression is a pure data transformation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation with no need for external command execution[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Violates RFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[39m**: The GZIP specification [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m defines GZIP as a data [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompression format with no provision for command execution[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Unprecedented in codebase**: No other compressor implementations [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mBZip2CompressorInputStream, XZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m execute OS commands[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No test coverage**: The test suite has no tests validating command execution [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior - all tests treat GZIP processing as pure data transformation[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Breaks proper control flow**: The malicious code is inserted between FCOMMENT [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m401[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and FHCRC checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m414[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, disrupting the RFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[39m-compliant[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader parsing sequence[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Obfuscated trigger**: The `[0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` condition is deliberately obfuscated to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhide malicious intent[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe legitimate GZIP header parsing flow that must be preserved:[0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m399[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m401[0m[39m: FCOMMENT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m parsing if present[0m                              [2m                [0m
